 in) Let us tell you that Railway Recruitment Board is conducting recruitment examination for 62 thousand 907 posts of Group d (RRB Group D)
 pariksha ke liye admit card (RRB Admit Card) exam se 4 din pehle jari kiye ja rahe hai
 The exam is scheduled to run till 17 December
 group di kii pehle charan kii pariksha main paas hone vaale ummidavaaron ko duusare charan kii shaareerik dakshata pariksha main baithne ko milegaa

 andhra pradesh se alag telugana rajya ke gathan kii ghoshnaa se judi ghatnaon kaa samayvaar byora:1948:bhartiya sena ne telugana sahit hyderabad riyasat ko bharat main milaayaa
 1 November 1956: Telangana was carved out of Madras State and included in Andhra State, a separate state for Telugu speakers was established
 1969:telugana ko pruthak rajya ghoshit karne ke liye 'jai telugana' andolan kii shuruyaat
 More than 300 people died in police firing
 1972:andhra pradesh ke tatavarti ilaakon main 'jai andhra' andolan kii shuruyaat
 1997: The Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) came out in support of Telangana, and contested the 1998 election with the slogan 'one vote, two states'
 2001:telugana andolat ko jivit rakhane ke liye ke
 Chandrasekhar Rao founded the Telangana Rashtra Samithi (TRS)
 2004:tiares ne congress ke saath sanyukt rup se chunaav main hissaa liya or paanch loksabhaa siton tathaa 26 vidhansabha siton par jeet darj kii
 The United Progressive Alliance (UPA) party included the Telangana issue in its Common Minimum Program and formed a three-member committee headed by Pranab Mukherjee

 February 3, 2010: Central government constitutes five-member Srikrishna Committee on Telangana issue
 28 disambar 2012:kendriya grahamantri susheel kumaar scindia ne ek sarvadaleey baithak ke baad ek maheene ke andar antim nirnay kiye jane kii ghoshnaa kii
